  IF(AND(NE(?b, NUM0), EQ(MOD(?a, ?b), NUM0)), MUL(PLUS(MUL(?x, DIV(?a, ?b)), ?y), ?b), PLUS(MUL(?x, ?a), MUL(?y, ?b))) -> PLUS(MUL(?x, ?a), MUL(?y, ?b))
  IF(AND(GT(NUM0, ?a), EQ(MOD(?b, ?a), NUM0)), MUL(MAX(?x, MUL(?y, DIV(?b, ?a))), ?a), MIN(MUL(?x, ?a), MUL(?y, ?b))) -> MIN(MUL(?x, ?a), MUL(?y, ?b))
